	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "尾崎…渚……。",
			NULL, "Nagisa... Ozaki...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//rトラックに轢かれて、……即死…っ！！
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "トラックに轢かれて、……即死…っ！！",
			NULL, "She was hit by a truck... and died immediately...!!", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	PlayBGM(2, "hm02_11", 128, 0);
	DrawScene("background/kuruma5_02", 250 );
	PlaySE(3, "tataku", 256, 64);
	ShakeScreen( 1, 15, 15, 2, 0, );

//巴rvS11/28/420101141.「……。kvS11/28/420101142.藤田くん、大至急で大牧に向かって」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#9d7f69>巴</color>", NULL, "<color=#9d7f69>Tomoe</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 28, "ps3/s11/28/420101141", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……。",
			NULL, "\"...", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 28, "ps3/s11/28/420101142", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "藤田くん、大至急で大牧に向かって」",
			NULL, "Fujita-kun, head for Oumaki right away.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//藤田rvS11/31/421200046.「えっ？」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#54636b>藤田</color>", NULL, "<color=#54636b>Fujita</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 31, "ps3/s11/31/421200046", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「えっ？」",
			NULL, "\"Huh?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//巴rvS11/28/420101143.「早くッッ！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#9d7f69>巴</color>", NULL, "<color=#9d7f69>Tomoe</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 28, "ps3/s11/28/420101143", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「早くッッ！！」",
			NULL, "\"Hurry!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(6, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/toki004", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 5000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
	DrawSceneWithMask("black", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );

}
